[19/01/24, 6:01:44‚ÄØPM] Samir Arora-President- NAR üáÆüá≥: Dear Friends & Esteemed Members of *CREA (I)*,

On behalf of all of us at CREA (I) Committee including all the Past Committee Members, I am honoured & thrilled to share an exciting news with all of you of a major milestone and one of our biggest dreams becoming a reality at CREA (I). 

I am overwhelmed with joy and gratitude as I announce the realization of a long-cherished dream ‚Äì our very own office for the Confederation of Real Estate Associates (India). This milestone is a testament to the collective dedication and unwavering commitment of each member. The new office will not only serve as a hub for collaboration and innovation but also symbolize our commitment to advancing the real estate industry. 

The journey leading to this moment has been marked by shared aspirations, challenges, and triumphs. On behalf of Chairman Emeritus and the Committee, I extend my heartfelt thanks to every member who played a pivotal role in making this dream a reality. Your passion and resilience have shaped not just the future of our association but also the landscape of our shared profession.

This new CREA (I) office, a prime address at Barton Centre on MG Road symbolizes not only a physical space but also a sanctuary for collaboration, innovation, and the continued growth of our community. Let it serve as a hub for exchanging ideas, fostering camaraderie, and advancing the standards of excellence we collectively uphold.

Yet, as we celebrate this achievement, let us also look forward with a renewed sense of purpose. The roadmap ahead is filled with opportunities to elevate our association and its members to greater heights. Let us strive for inclusivity, embrace innovation, and remain united in our commitment to excellence.

Together, we embark on a journey that transcends brick and mortar ‚Äì a journey that defines the very essence of our association. As we navigate the path ahead, let the spirit of collaboration guide us, and let our shared vision be the compass that steers us towards a future filled with success and prosperity.

Thank you for being an integral part of this extraordinary journey. As I keep saying, from Ordinary to Extraordinary, it is just that Extra that makes our Association and all of you members Extraordinary. 

The visionary leader, our charismatic Chairman Emeritus, Mr. Pradeep Joe gave us this wonderful platform and forum called CREA (I). Some of us along with him dared to dream big and a few years back we aligned our Goals to the Dream of CREA (I) owning an office in CBD in Bangalore which every CREA (I) member can be proud of. The National Convention and many a other journey have been an effort aligned with that Dream and today Pradeep Joe, myself, all Committee members (past and present) are proud to say, *Dreams do come True*. All we need is courage, determination, focus and a will to succeed. 

And mark my words. The New Milestone, the landmark, the CREA (I) Office is just the beginning of new goals we all need to achieve together because all of us at CREA (I) dare to Dream. 

Abhi udaan baaki hai,
Abhi to naapi hai sirf muthi bhar zameen,
Abhi to pura Aasman baaki hai !

Long live CREA (I)

With gratitude,
Best wishes
On behalf of CREA (I) Committee

Samir Arora
Proudest member of CREA (I) today and also
Chairman & Past President
